SELECT *, `a`.`number` as `spb_number`, `f`.`number` as `inv_number`
FROM `od_spb_doc` as `a`
JOIN `od_ba_stat` as `b` ON `a`.`spb_status`=`b`.`stat_id`
JOIN `od_user_level` as `c` ON `a`.`ul_id`=`c`.`id`
JOIN `od_partner` as `d` ON `a`.`partner_id`=`d`.`partner_id`
JOIN `od_spb_mod` as `e` ON `a`.`spb_id`=`e`.`spb_id`
JOIN `od_inv_doc` as `f` ON `e`.`inv_id`=`f`.`inv_id`
JOIN `od_partner_bank` as `g` ON `a`.`partner_id`=`g`.`partner_id`
JOIN `od_partner_mod` as `h` ON `a`.`partner_id`=`h`.`partner_id`
JOIN `od_user` as `i` ON `h`.`user_id`=`i`.`id`
JOIN `od_inv_mod` as `j` ON `j`.`inv_id`=`j`.`inv_id`
JOIN `od_ba_doc` as `k` ON `k`.`ba_id`=`k`.`ba_id`
WHERE `a`.`spb_id` = '3'
AND `c`.`status` = 1
ORDER BY `a`.`spb_id` DESC
